## Instruction

You need to read the inventory levels of WooCommerce products, check the current stock quantity (stock_quantity) for each product against the safety threshold (stock_threshold), identify all products with stock below the threshold, and automatically update a Google Sheets purchase requisition list named stock_sheet. For each low-stock product, record it in Google Sheets and send an email notification to the purchasing manager (the email address is in purchasing_manager_email.txt). You need to find all low-stock products, record them and send emails. The email template can be found in stock_alert_email_template.md.

## Initial State

### Local Workspace

<div className="file-tree">
<a href="https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/release_v1/tasks/finalpool/woocommerce-stock-alert/initial_workspace">workspace</a>/
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ purchasing_manager_email.txt
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ stock_alert_email_template.md
</div>

### Google Sheet

<div className="file-tree">
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ <a href="https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/19q_G5MMKpfRIblnR3_4613BtQDuFR0lNIE7UqsW7nbg">stock_sheet</a>
</div>

### WooCommerce

You can review the data construction process during testing [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/release_v1/tasks/finalpool/woocommerce-stock-alert/preprocess).

```json output_result
# Stock Alert Email Template

## Email Subject
[Stock Alert] {product_name} Stock Below Safety Threshold

## Email Body

Dear Purchasing Manager,

The system has detected that the following product's stock level is below the safety threshold. Please take immediate action:

## Product Information
- **Product Name**: {product_name}
- **SKU**: {sku}
- **Current Stock**: {current_stock}
- **Safety Threshold**: {threshold}
- **Supplier**: {supplier_name}
- **Supplier Contact**: {supplier_contact}

## Action Required
Please review the stock levels and consider placing a purchase order to replenish inventory.

For detailed information and to update the purchase requisition list, please visit the Google Sheets link: {google_sheets_link}

Best regards,
Stock Alert System

```

```python

import json
from datetime import datetime

# Product data from WooCommerce
products_data = [
  {"id": 21, "name": "LG OLED 77-inch C4", "sku": "LG-OLED-C4-77", "stock_quantity": 8, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "4"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "LG Electronics", "contact": "b2b@lg.com", "supplier_id": "SUP012"}}]},
  {"id": 20, "name": "Bose QuietComfort Ultra", "sku": "BOSE-QC-ULTRA", "stock_quantity": 22, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "10"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Bose Professional", "contact": "wholesale@bose.com", "supplier_id": "SUP011"}}]},
  {"id": 19, "name": "Sony Alpha 7R V Camera", "sku": "SONY-A7R5", "stock_quantity": 15, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "6"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Sony Professional Imaging", "contact": "pro-imaging@sony.com", "supplier_id": "SUP010"}}]},
  {"id": 18, "name": "Nintendo Switch OLED", "sku": "NINTENDO-SWITCH-OLED", "stock_quantity": 2, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "12"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Nintendo Distribution", "contact": "orders@nintendo-dist.com", "supplier_id": "SUP009"}}]},
  {"id": 17, "name": "MacBook Pro 14-inch M3", "sku": "MACBOOK-PRO-14-M3", "stock_quantity": 3, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "8"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Apple Corporate Sales", "contact": "corporate@apple.com", "supplier_id": "SUP008"}}]},
  {"id": 16, "name": "Microsoft Surface Pro 9", "sku": "MS-SURFACE-PRO9", "stock_quantity": 1, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "6"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Microsoft China", "contact": "surface@microsoft.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP007"}}]},
  {"id": 15, "name": "Canon EOS R6", "sku": "CANON-EOS-R6", "stock_quantity": 4, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "8"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Canon Professional", "contact": "pro@canon.com.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP006"}}]},
  {"id": 14, "name": "iPad Air 5th Gen", "sku": "IPAD-AIR-5", "stock_quantity": 7, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "12"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Apple Authorized Distributor", "contact": "sales@apple-distributor.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP002"}}]},
  {"id": 13, "name": "Logitech MX Master 3S", "sku": "LOGI-MX-MASTER3S", "stock_quantity": 18, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "10"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Logitech China", "contact": "wholesale@logitech.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP005"}}]},
  {"id": 12, "name": "Samsung 65\" QLED TV", "sku": "SAMSUNG-Q80B-65", "stock_quantity": 2, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "5"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Samsung Display", "contact": "b2b@samsung.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP004"}}]},
  {"id": 11, "name": "Sony WH-1000XM5 Headphones", "sku": "SONY-WH1000XM5", "stock_quantity": 25, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "20"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Sony Electronics", "contact": "order@sony-electronics.com", "supplier_id": "SUP003"}}]},
  {"id": 10, "name": "iPhone 15 Pro", "sku": "IPHONE-15-PRO", "stock_quantity": 3, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "15"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Apple Authorized Distributor", "contact": "sales@apple-distributor.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP002"}}]},
  {"id": 9, "name": "Laptop Dell XPS 13", "sku": "DELL-XPS-13", "stock_quantity": 5, "meta_data": [{"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "10"}, {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Dell China", "contact": "supplier@dell.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP001"}}]}
]

# Process each product and identify low stock items
low_stock_products = []

for product in products_data:
    # Extract stock threshold
    stock_threshold = None
    supplier_info = None
    
    for meta in product['meta_data']:
        if meta['key'] == 'stock_threshold':
            stock_threshold = int(meta['value'])
        elif meta['key'] == 'supplier':
            supplier_info = meta['value']
    
    # Check if stock is below threshold
    if stock_threshold and product['stock_quantity'] < stock_threshold:
        # Calculate suggested order quantity (to reach threshold + 50% buffer)
        suggested_qty = int((stock_threshold * 1.5) - product['stock_quantity'])
        
        low_stock_products.append({
            'product_id': product['id'],
            'product_name': product['name'],
            'sku': product['sku'],
            'current_stock': product['stock_quantity'],
            'threshold': stock_threshold,
            'supplier_name': supplier_info['name'] if supplier_info else 'N/A',
            'supplier_id': supplier_info['supplier_id'] if supplier_info else 'N/A',
            'supplier_contact': supplier_info['contact'] if supplier_info else 'N/A',
            'suggested_order_qty': suggested_qty
        })

print(f"Found {len(low_stock_products)} products with low stock:\n")
for item in low_stock_products:
    print(f"- {item['product_name']} (SKU: {item['sku']})")
    print(f"  Current: {item['current_stock']}, Threshold: {item['threshold']}")
    print(f"  Supplier: {item['supplier_name']}")
    print()

# Save to JSON for later use
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/low_stock_products.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(low_stock_products, f, indent=2)

print(f"\nTotal low-stock products: {len(low_stock_products)}")
 code
```

```python

import json
from datetime import datetime

# Load low stock products
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/low_stock_products.json', 'r') as f:
    low_stock_products = json.load(f)

# Prepare data for Google Sheets (starting from row 2 since row 1 is headers)
# Format: Product ID, Product Name, SKU, Current Stock, Safety Threshold, Supplier Name, Supplier ID, Supplier Contact, Alert Time, Suggested Order Quantity
sheet_data = []
current_time = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

for product in low_stock_products:
    row = [
        str(product['product_id']),
        product['product_name'],
        product['sku'],
        product['current_stock'],
        str(product['threshold']),
        product['supplier_name'],
        product['supplier_id'],
        product['supplier_contact'],
        current_time,
        str(product['suggested_order_qty'])
    ]
    sheet_data.append(row)

# Save sheet data for batch update
print(f"Prepared {len(sheet_data)} rows for Google Sheets update")
print("\nSheet data preview:")
for i, row in enumerate(sheet_data[:3], 1):
    print(f"Row {i}: {row}")

with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/sheet_update_data.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(sheet_data, f, indent=2)

print(f"\n‚úì Sheet data saved to sheet_update_data.json")
```

```python

import json

# Load data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/low_stock_products.json', 'r') as f:
    low_stock_products = json.load(f)

# Load email template
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/stock_alert_email_template.md', 'r') as f:
    template = f.read()

# Load purchasing manager email
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/purchasing_manager_email.txt', 'r') as f:
    manager_email = f.read().strip()

print(f"Purchasing Manager Email: {manager_email}")
print(f"Total products to send alerts for: {len(low_stock_products)}")

# Google Sheets link
google_sheets_link = "https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1Zd7vvozgV8TtYHl_Nbq4BhZPsGzh5PkYJAHY5G2GlIM"

# Prepare email data for each product
emails_to_send = []

for product in low_stock_products:
    # Extract subject from template
    subject_line = template.split('\n')[2]  # Line with subject
    subject = subject_line.replace('[Stock Alert] {product_name} Stock Below Safety Threshold', 
                                  f"[Stock Alert] {product['product_name']} Stock Below Safety Threshold")
    
    # Prepare email body
    body = template.split('## Email Body')[1].strip()
    
    # Replace placeholders
    body = body.replace('{product_name}', product['product_name'])
    body = body.replace('{sku}', product['sku'])
    body = body.replace('{current_stock}', str(product['current_stock']))
    body = body.replace('{threshold}', str(product['threshold']))
    body = body.replace('{supplier_name}', product['supplier_name'])
    body = body.replace('{supplier_contact}', product['supplier_contact'])
    body = body.replace('{google_sheets_link}', google_sheets_link)
    
    emails_to_send.append({
        'to': manager_email,
        'subject': subject,
        'body': body,
        'product_name': product['product_name']
    })

# Save email data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/emails_to_send.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(emails_to_send, f, indent=2)

print(f"\n‚úì Prepared {len(emails_to_send)} emails")
print("\nFirst email preview:")
print(f"To: {emails_to_send[0]['to']}")
print(f"Subject: {emails_to_send[0]['subject']}")
print(f"Body (first 200 chars): {emails_to_send[0]['body'][:200]}...")
 code
```

```python

import json

# Load data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/low_stock_products.json', 'r') as f:
    low_stock_products = json.load(f)

# Load purchasing manager email
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/purchasing_manager_email.txt', 'r') as f:
    manager_email = f.read().strip()

# Google Sheets link
google_sheets_link = "https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1Zd7vvozgV8TtYHl_Nbq4BhZPsGzh5PkYJAHY5G2GlIM"

# Email template content (from the file)
email_body_template = """Dear Purchasing Manager,

The system has detected that the following product's stock level is below the safety threshold. Please take immediate action:

## Product Information
- **Product Name**: {product_name}
- **SKU**: {sku}
- **Current Stock**: {current_stock}
- **Safety Threshold**: {threshold}
- **Supplier**: {supplier_name}
- **Supplier Contact**: {supplier_contact}

## Action Required
Please review the stock levels and consider placing a purchase order to replenish inventory.

For detailed information and to update the purchase requisition list, please visit the Google Sheets link: {google_sheets_link}

Best regards,
Stock Alert System
"""

# Prepare email data for each product
emails_to_send = []

for product in low_stock_products:
    subject = f"[Stock Alert] {product['product_name']} Stock Below Safety Threshold"
    
    # Prepare email body
    body = email_body_template.format(
        product_name=product['product_name'],
        sku=product['sku'],
        current_stock=product['current_stock'],
        threshold=product['threshold'],
        supplier_name=product['supplier_name'],
        supplier_contact=product['supplier_contact'],
        google_sheets_link=google_sheets_link
    )
    
    emails_to_send.append({
        'to': manager_email,
        'subject': subject,
        'body': body,
        'product_name': product['product_name']
    })

# Save email data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/emails_to_send.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(emails_to_send, f, indent=2)

print(f"‚úì Prepared {len(emails_to_send)} emails for {manager_email}\n")
print("Email subjects:")
for i, email in enumerate(emails_to_send, 1):
    print(f"{i}. {email['subject']}")
 code
```

```json output_result
3. [Stock Alert] Microsoft Surface Pro 9 Stock Below Safety Threshold
```

```python

import json

# Load email data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/emails_to_send.json', 'r') as f:
    emails = json.load(f)

# Print the emails that will be sent
print(f"Ready to send {len(emails)} emails to {emails[0]['to']}\n")
for i, email in enumerate(emails, 1):
    print(f"{i}. {email['product_name']}")

# Save email commands for execution
print("\n" + "="*60)
print("Emails prepared and ready to send!")
 code
```

```python

import json

# Load the low stock products
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/low_stock_products.json', 'r') as f:
    low_stock_products = json.load(f)

# Create summary report
report = """
================================================================================
                    INVENTORY STOCK ALERT SYSTEM - SUMMARY REPORT
================================================================================

TASK COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY

Date: 2025-10-17 23:17:23
Purchasing Manager: laura_thompson@mcp.com
Google Sheets: https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1Zd7vvozgV8TtYHl_Nbq4BhZPsGzh5PkYJAHY5G2GlIM

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
SUMMARY
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Total Products Scanned: 13
Products Below Safety Threshold: 8
Google Sheets Records Updated: 8
Email Notifications Sent: 8

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
LOW STOCK PRODUCTS IDENTIFIED
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
"""

for i, product in enumerate(low_stock_products, 1):
    report += f"""
{i}. {product['product_name']}
   SKU: {product['sku']}
   Product ID: {product['product_id']}
   Current Stock: {product['current_stock']} units
   Safety Threshold: {product['threshold']} units
   Stock Deficit: {product['threshold'] - product['current_stock']} units
   Suggested Order Quantity: {product['suggested_order_qty']} units
   Supplier: {product['supplier_name']} ({product['supplier_id']})
   Supplier Contact: {product['supplier_contact']}
   Status: ‚úì Recorded in Google Sheets
   Email Alert: ‚úì Sent to purchasing manager
"""

report += """
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
ACTIONS TAKEN
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
1. ‚úì Retrieved all WooCommerce products (13 products)
2. ‚úì Analyzed stock levels against safety thresholds
3. ‚úì Identified 8 products below safety threshold
4. ‚úì Updated Google Sheets purchase requisition list with all 8 products
5. ‚úì Sent 8 individual email notifications to laura_thompson@mcp.com
6. ‚úì Included supplier information and Google Sheets link in each email

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
PRODUCTS WITH ADEQUATE STOCK (No Action Required)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
"""

adequate_stock = [
    "LG OLED 77-inch C4 (8/4 units)",
    "Bose QuietComfort Ultra (22/10 units)",
    "Sony Alpha 7R V Camera (15/6 units)",
    "Logitech MX Master 3S (18/10 units)",
    "Sony WH-1000XM5 Headphones (25/20 units)"
]

for item in adequate_stock:
    report += f"‚Ä¢ {item}\n"

report += """
================================================================================
                            END OF REPORT
================================================================================
"""

print(report)

# Save report to file
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/stock_alert_report.txt', 'w') as f:
    f.write(report)

print("\n‚úì Report saved to stock_alert_report.txt")
 code
```

```json output_result
# Stock Alert Email Template

## Email Subject
[Stock Alert] {product_name} Stock Below Safety Threshold

## Email Body

Dear Purchasing Manager,

The system has detected that the following product's stock level is below the safety threshold. Please take immediate action:

## Product Information
- **Product Name**: {product_name}
- **SKU**: {sku}
- **Current Stock**: {current_stock}
- **Safety Threshold**: {threshold}
- **Supplier**: {supplier_name}
- **Supplier Contact**: {supplier_contact}

## Action Required
Please review the stock levels and consider placing a purchase order to replenish inventory.

For detailed information and to update the purchase requisition list, please visit the Google Sheets link: {google_sheets_link}

Best regards,
Stock Alert System
```

```python
import json
from datetime import datetime

# Parse the WooCommerce products data
products_data = [
    {
        "id": 21,
        "name": "LG OLED 77-inch C4",
        "sku": "LG-OLED-C4-77",
        "stock_quantity": 8,
        "stock_threshold": 4,
        "supplier": {"name": "LG Electronics", "contact": "b2b@lg.com", "supplier_id": "SUP012"}
    },
    {
        "id": 20,
        "name": "Bose QuietComfort Ultra",
        "sku": "BOSE-QC-ULTRA",
        "stock_quantity": 22,
        "stock_threshold": 10,
        "supplier": {"name": "Bose Professional", "contact": "wholesale@bose.com", "supplier_id": "SUP011"}
    },
    {
        "id": 19,
        "name": "Sony Alpha 7R V Camera",
        "sku": "SONY-A7R5",
        "stock_quantity": 15,
        "stock_threshold": 6,
        "supplier": {"name": "Sony Professional Imaging", "contact": "pro-imaging@sony.com", "supplier_id": "SUP010"}
    },
    {
        "id": 18,
        "name": "Nintendo Switch OLED",
        "sku": "NINTENDO-SWITCH-OLED",
        "stock_quantity": 2,
        "stock_threshold": 12,
        "supplier": {"name": "Nintendo Distribution", "contact": "orders@nintendo-dist.com", "supplier_id": "SUP009"}
    },
    {
        "id": 17,
        "name": "MacBook Pro 14-inch M3",
        "sku": "MACBOOK-PRO-14-M3",
        "stock_quantity": 3,
        "stock_threshold": 8,
        "supplier": {"name": "Apple Corporate Sales", "contact": "corporate@apple.com", "supplier_id": "SUP008"}
    },
    {
        "id": 16,
        "name": "Microsoft Surface Pro 9",
        "sku": "MS-SURFACE-PRO9",
        "stock_quantity": 1,
        "stock_threshold": 6,
        "supplier": {"name": "Microsoft China", "contact": "surface@microsoft.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP007"}
    },
    {
        "id": 15,
        "name": "Canon EOS R6",
        "sku": "CANON-EOS-R6",
        "stock_quantity": 4,
        "stock_threshold": 8,
        "supplier": {"name": "Canon Professional", "contact": "pro@canon.com.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP006"}
    },
    {
        "id": 14,
        "name": "iPad Air 5th Gen",
        "sku": "IPAD-AIR-5",
        "stock_quantity": 7,
        "stock_threshold": 12,
        "supplier": {"name": "Apple Authorized Distributor", "contact": "sales@apple-distributor.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP002"}
    },
    {
        "id": 13,
        "name": "Logitech MX Master 3S",
        "sku": "LOGI-MX-MASTER3S",
        "stock_quantity": 18,
        "stock_threshold": 10,
        "supplier": {"name": "Logitech China", "contact": "wholesale@logitech.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP005"}
    },
    {
        "id": 12,
        "name": "Samsung 65\" QLED TV",
        "sku": "SAMSUNG-Q80B-65",
        "stock_quantity": 2,
        "stock_threshold": 5,
        "supplier": {"name": "Samsung Display", "contact": "b2b@samsung.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP004"}
    },
    {
        "id": 11,
        "name": "Sony WH-1000XM5 Headphones",
        "sku": "SONY-WH1000XM5",
        "stock_quantity": 25,
        "stock_threshold": 20,
        "supplier": {"name": "Sony Electronics", "contact": "order@sony-electronics.com", "supplier_id": "SUP003"}
    },
    {
        "id": 10,
        "name": "iPhone 15 Pro",
        "sku": "IPHONE-15-PRO",
        "stock_quantity": 3,
        "stock_threshold": 15,
        "supplier": {"name": "Apple Authorized Distributor", "contact": "sales@apple-distributor.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP002"}
    },
    {
        "id": 9,
        "name": "Laptop Dell XPS 13",
        "sku": "DELL-XPS-13",
        "stock_quantity": 5,
        "stock_threshold": 10,
        "supplier": {"name": "Dell China", "contact": "supplier@dell.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP001"}
    }
]

# Identify low-stock products
low_stock_products = []
for product in products_data:
    if product["stock_quantity"] < product["stock_threshold"]:
        # Calculate suggested order quantity (threshold - current stock + buffer)
        suggested_order = product["stock_threshold"] - product["stock_quantity"] + 5  # Add 5 as buffer
        
        low_stock_products.append({
            "product_id": product["id"],
            "product_name": product["name"],
            "sku": product["sku"],
            "current_stock": product["stock_quantity"],
            "safety_threshold": product["stock_threshold"],
            "supplier_name": product["supplier"]["name"],
            "supplier_id": product["supplier"]["supplier_id"],
            "supplier_contact": product["supplier"]["contact"],
            "suggested_order_quantity": suggested_order,
            "alert_time": datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
        })

print("Low-stock products identified:")
print(f"Total low-stock products: {len(low_stock_products)}")
print("\n" + "="*80)

for product in low_stock_products:
    print(f"Product: {product['product_name']}")
    print(f"  SKU: {product['sku']}")
    print(f"  Current Stock: {product['current_stock']}")
    print(f"  Safety Threshold: {product['safety_threshold']}")
    print(f"  Supplier: {product['supplier_name']}")
    print(f"  Suggested Order Quantity: {product['suggested_order_quantity']}")
    print("-" * 40)

# Prepare data for Google Sheets
sheets_data = []
for product in low_stock_products:
    sheets_data.append([
        str(product["product_id"]),
        product["product_name"],
        product["sku"],
        str(product["current_stock"]),
        str(product["safety_threshold"]),
        product["supplier_name"],
        product["supplier_id"],
        product["supplier_contact"],
        product["alert_time"],
        str(product["suggested_order_quantity"])
    ])

print(f"\nPrepared {len(sheets_data)} rows for Google Sheets update")

# Save the data for use in the next steps
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/low_stock_products.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump({"low_stock_products": low_stock_products, "sheets_data": sheets_data}, f, indent=2)

print("\nData saved to low_stock_products.json") code
```

```python
import json

# Load the low stock products data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/low_stock_products.json', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)

sheets_data = data['sheets_data']

print(f"Preparing to update Google Sheets with {len(sheets_data)} low-stock products")
print("\nData to be added:")
for i, row in enumerate(sheets_data, 1):
    print(f"Row {i}: {row}")

# Prepare the range for update (starting from row 3)
start_row = 3
end_row = start_row + len(sheets_data) - 1
range_str = f"A{start_row}:J{end_row}"

print(f"\nUpdate range: {range_str}")

# Save the range info for the next step
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/sheets_update_info.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump({
        "sheets_data": sheets_data,
        "range": range_str,
        "start_row": start_row,
        "end_row": end_row
    }, f, indent=2)

print("\nUpdate information saved to sheets_update_info.json") code
```

```python
import json

# Load the low stock products data
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/low_stock_products.json', 'r') as f:
    data = json.load(f)

low_stock_products = data['low_stock_products']

# Read the purchasing manager email
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/purchasing_manager_email.txt', 'r') as f:
    purchasing_manager_email = f.read().strip()

print(f"Purchasing Manager Email: {purchasing_manager_email}")
print(f"\nPreparing to send {len(low_stock_products)} email notifications")

# Google Sheets link
google_sheets_link = "https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1iKxA5v_-Q5p4idUGLyDm4Ke_o0WW029yxDZrvRLA2qo/edit"

# Prepare email data for each product
email_data = []
for product in low_stock_products:
    subject = f"[Stock Alert] {product['product_name']} Stock Below Safety Threshold"
    
    body = f"""Dear Purchasing Manager,

The system has detected that the following product's stock level is below the safety threshold. Please take immediate action:

## Product Information
- **Product Name**: {product['product_name']}
- **SKU**: {product['sku']}
- **Current Stock**: {product['current_stock']}
- **Safety Threshold**: {product['safety_threshold']}
- **Supplier**: {product['supplier_name']}
- **Supplier Contact**: {product['supplier_contact']}

## Action Required
Please review the stock levels and consider placing a purchase order to replenish inventory.

For detailed information and to update the purchase requisition list, please visit the Google Sheets link: {google_sheets_link}

Best regards,
Stock Alert System
"""
    
    email_data.append({
        "product_name": product['product_name'],
        "to": purchasing_manager_email,
        "subject": subject,
        "body": body
    })

print("\nEmail data prepared:")
for i, email in enumerate(email_data, 1):
    print(f"\nEmail {i}: {email['product_name']}")
    print(f"Subject: {email['subject']}")
    print(f"Body preview: {email['body'][:100]}...")

# Save email data for sending
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/email_data.json', 'w') as f:
    json.dump(email_data, f, indent=2)

print(f"\nEmail data saved to email_data.json") code
```
